</script><script id="7635cfce31ce270fe52adb7e4ecd85ad-1" type="nitropack/inlinescript" class="nitropack-inline-script">
                    document.addEventListener("gform/post_init", function() {
                        // Find all month dropdowns within Gravity Forms
                        document.querySelectorAll('.gfield_date_dropdown_month select').forEach(function(select) {
                            const months = ["", "Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun", "Jul", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec"];

                            select.querySelectorAll("option").forEach(function(option, index) {
                                if (index > 0) { // Skip the first empty option
                                    option.text = months[index];
                                }
                            });
                        });
                    });


                    document.addEventListener("gform/post_init", function() {
                        const yearDropdown = document.querySelector("#input_9_74_3, #input_11_74_3, #input_12_74_3, #input_13_74_3");
                        if (yearDropdown) {
                            const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                            yearDropdown.innerHTML = ""; // Clear existing options

                            for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                                const year = currentYear + i;
                                let option = document.createElement("option");
                                option.value = year;
                                option.textContent = year;
                                yearDropdown.appendChild(option);
                            }
                        }
                    });

                    
                    document.addEventListener('gform/post_init', function () {
                        // Listen for clicks on "Next" buttons
                        document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                            if (e.target && e.target.id === 'gform_next_button_12_61') {
                                const form = e.target.closest('form');
                                
                                // Target your required field (adjust selector)
                                const requiredFields = form.querySelectorAll('input[name="input_127_phone"]');

                                let allFilled = true;
                                requiredFields.forEach(field => {
                                    if (!field.value.trim()) {
                                        allFilled = false;
                                    }

                                     if(field && field.getAttribute("type") === "tel") {
                                        const validationMessage = field.closest('.ginput_container_phone').querySelector('.gfipm-error-msg');
                                        console.log("Validation message:", validationMessage);
                                        if (validationMessage) {
                                            allFilled = false;
                                        }
                                    }

                                });

                                if (!allFilled) {
                                    e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                                    e.preventDefault(); // Stop going to next page
                                }
                            }
                        }, true);
                    });

  "> <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-af0c4d71 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex"> <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis: 47%;"> <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-large-font-size">safari is a more <mark style="background-color: rgba(0,0,0,0);" class="has-inline-color has-primary-color">intense</mark>, authentic and positive way to travel</h2> </div> <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis: 53%;"> <p>If you haven’t yet been on a proper safari, then you’re in for a real treat. At its best, a safari can be a genuinely deep and life punctuating event.</p> <p>But organising a great safari is not straightforward, it needs to be done with care, precision and expertise. That&#8217;s where we come in.</p> <p>If wildlife is your primary focus, the key will be the quality and the tonality of each encounter. There is a world of difference between an intimate one-to-one encounter with a lion and being parked in an ugly circle of vehicles. We can and will deliver that difference.</p> <p>A great safari is a sequence of magical moments, many of which are only peripherally related to the main event. Even on a conventional savanna safari, the wildlife is perhaps only a quarter of the total experience.</p> <p>As we help you plan your safari, we consider the flow of every single day, to facilitate the spontaneous emergence of these moments. We do this by carefully blending a wide range of quality ingredients, such as wonderful landscapes, carefully considered lodges, unusual activities, passionate people and impromptu encounters.</p> <p>This considered way of travel, this attitude, isn’t only applicable to wildlife experiences. We can create safaris to the historic sites of Egypt, self-drive explorations through the deserts of Namibia or cultural adventures in Rajasthan and Bhutan. We can even bring our safari approach to bear on trips to Antarctica.</p> </div> </div> </div> </section> <section x-data="wideImageWithText(2)" class="Wide__Image__With__Text relative flex justify-end padding-top-md" x-intersect.once.threshold.25="visible = true;"> <div class="Wide__Image__With__Text-container flex flex-col items-start -right"> <div class="mb-10 text-left transition ease-in-out duration-1000" :class="visible ? We have to live up to that standard every single day, every single trip.</p> <p>Our intimate team has an incredible amount of first hand experience, knowledge and expertise.
